f'{DAILY_SUMMARIES_PREFIX}{d.isoformat()}.parquet'\n254\t\n255\t\n256\tdef _produce_daily_summary(d: date,\n257\t                           email_aliases: dict, login_aliases: dict) -> bool:\n258\t    \"\"\"\n259\t    Read one day's raw commits + tools via DuckDB httpfs, compute per-user stats,\n260\t    write compact summary.  Returns True if summary was written.\n261\t    \"\"\"\n262\t    os.makedirs(SPILL_DIR, exist_ok=True)\n263\t    con = duckdb.connect(':memory:')\n264\t    con.execute(\"SET \"\"\"\n298\t\n299\t    tools_tbl = None\n300\t    try:\n301\t        tools_tbl = con.execute(tools_sql).fetch_arrow_table()\n302\t    except Exception:\n303\t        pass\n304\t\n305\t    if tools_tbl is not None and tools_tbl.num_rows > 0:\n306\t        con.register('tools', tools_tbl)\n307\t        q = \"\"\"\n308\t        WITH tl AS (\n309\t            SELECT c.username, t.tool_name, COUNT(*) AS cnt\n310\t            FROM commits c JOIN tools t USING (sha)\n311\t            GROUP BY c.username, t.tool_name\n312\t        ),\n313\t        tj AS (\n314\t            SELECT username, to_json(map(list(tool_name), list(cnt))) AS tc\n315\t            FROM tl GROUP BY username\n316\t        ),\n317\t        ai AS (\n318\t            SELECT c.username, COUNT(DISTINCT c.sha) AS ai_cnt\n319\t            FROM commits c JOIN tools t USING (sha)\n320\t            GROUP BY c.username\n321\t        )\n322\t        SELECT c.username,\n323\t               CAST(COUNT(*) AS INT) AS commit_count,\n324\t               CAST(COALESCE(a.ai_cnt, 0) AS INT) AS ai_count,\n325\t               list(DISTINCT c.repo) AS repos,\n326\t               COALESCE(tj.tc, '{}') AS tool_counts,\n327\t               MIN(c.committed_at) AS first_at,\n328\t               MAX(c.committed_at) AS last_at\n329\t        FROM commits c\n330\t        LEFT JOIN tj USING (username)\n331\t        LEFT JOIN ai AS a USING (username)\n332\t        GROUP BY c.username, tj.tc, a.ai_cnt\n333\t        \"\"\"\n334\t    else:\n335\t        q = \"\"\"\n336\t        SELECT username,\n337\t               CAST(COUNT(*) AS INT) AS commit_count,\n338\t               CAST(0 AS INT) AS ai_count,\n339\t               list(DISTINCT repo) AS repos,\n340\t               '{}' AS tool_counts,\n341\t               MIN(committed_at) AS first_at,\n342\t               MAX(committed_at) AS last_at\n343\t        FROM commits\n344\t        GROUP BY username\n345\t        \"\"\"\n346\t\n347\t    result = 'state/backfill_cursor.txt'\n647\t\n648\t\n649\tdef _get_backfill_cursor() -> date | None:\n650\t    \"\"\"Read the cursor date from S3 (persists across pod restarts).\"\"\"\n651\t    data = backfill_daily_summaries(email_aliases: dict, login_aliases: dict,\n665\t                              max_days: int = BACKFILL_DAYS_PER_CYCLE) -> int:\n666\t    \"\"\"\n667\t    Produce daily summaries for historical dates that don't have one yet.\n668\t    Uses an S3-persisted cursor so the window advances on every cycle even\n669\t    when no data is found, avoiding the infinite-retry-same-dates bug.\n670\t    Returns the number of summaries produced.\n671\t    \"\"\"\n672\t    today = date.today()\n673\t    floor = date(2010, 1, 1)\n674\t\n675\t    cursor = _get_backfill_cursor()\n676\t    if cursor is None:\n677\t        # Start just before the 30d window; run_aggregation handles that window\n678\t        cursor = today - timedelta(days=32)\n679\t\n680\t    to_try: list[date] = []\n681\t    d = cursor\n682\t    while len(to_try) < max_days and d >= floor:\n683\t        to_try.append(d)\n684\t        d -= timedelta(days=1)\n685\t\n686\t    if not to_try:\n687\t        log.info('backfill: reached floor %s, nothing more to do', floor)\n688\t        return 0\n689\t\n690\t    log.info('backfill: trying %d dates (newest: %s, oldest: %s)',\n691\t             len(to_try), to_try[0], to_try[-1])\n692\t    produced = 0\n693\t    for d in to_try:\n694\t        try:\n695\t            if _produce_daily_summary(d, email_aliases, login_aliases):\n696\t                produced += 1\n697\t        except Exception:\n698\t            log.exception('backfill: failed to produce summary for %s', d)\n699\t\n700\t    # Advance cursor regardless of whether data was found\n701\t    new_cursor = to_try[-1] - timedelta(days=1)\n702\t    if new_cursor >= floor:\n703\t        _set_backfill_cursor(new_cursor)\n704\t\n705\t    log.info('backfill: produced %d/%d summaries, cursor → %s',\n706\t             produced, len(to_try), new_cursor)\n707\t    return produced\n708\t\n709\t\n710\t# ── Compaction (removed) ───────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n711\t# The compact_partitions() function has been removed.  With DuckDB httpfs and\n712\t# the ARMOR date fix (proper UTC timestamps), we no longer need to manually\n713\t# merge and deduplicate partitions.  DuckDB's read_parquet() handles filtering\n714\t# and deduplication efficiently.\n715\t\n716\t# ── Purge invalid parquets ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n717\t\n718\tdef _partition_key(obj_key: str):\n719\t    parts = obj_key.split('/')\n720\t    try:\n721\t        year  = int(next(p.split('=')[1] for p in parts if p.startswith('year=')))\n722\t        month = int(next(p.split('=')[1] for p in parts if p.startswith('month=')))\n723\t        day   = int(next(p.split('=')[1] for p in parts if p.startswith('day=')))\n724\t        return date(year, month, day)\n725\t    except (StopIteration, ValueError, IndexError):\n726\t        return None\n727\t\n728\t\n729\tdef _check_one_parquet(key: str) -> tuple[str, bool, str]:\n730\t    \"\"\"\n731\t    Return (key, is_bad, reason).\n732\t    Only marks a file bad for a confirmed schema error (committed_at is not a\n733\t    timestamp).  Read errors (network, ARMOR down) are NOT treated as bad.\n734\t    \"\"\"\n735\t    data = _s3_download_key(key)\n736\t    if data is None:\n737\t        return key, False, 'read error (skipped)'\n738\t    try:\n739\t        schema = pq.read_schema(io.BytesIO(data))\n740\t        if 'committed_at' in schema.names and not pa.types.is_timestamp(\n741\t            schema.field('committed_at').type\n742\t        ):\n743\t            return key, True, f'committed_at type={schema.field(\"committed_at\").type}'\n744\t        return key, False, ''\n745\t    except Exception as e:\n746\t        return key, False, f'read error (skipped): {e}'\n747\t\n748\t\n749\tdef purge_invalid_parquets() -> int:\n750\t    \"\"\"Full-corpus schema scan — delete files where ThreadPoolExecutor(max_workers=32) as pool:\n759\t        futures = [pool.submit(_check_one_parquet, k) for k in parquet_keys]\n760\t        for fut in as_completed(futures):\n761\t            key,        import boto3\n771\t        import botocore.config\n772\t        s3 = boto3.client(\n773\t            's3',\n774\t            endpoint_url=S3_ENDPOINT,\n775\t            aws_access_key_id=S3_KEY,\n776\t            aws_secret_access_key=S3_SECRET,\n777\t            region_name='auto',\n778\t            config=botocore.config.Config(max_pool_connections=10),\n779\t        )\n780\t        removed = 0\n781\t        for i in range(0, len(victims), 1000):\n782\t            batch = victims[i:i + 1000]\n783\t            resp = s3.delete_objects(\n784\t                Bucket=S3_BUCKET,\n785\t                Delete={'Objects': [{'Key': k} for k in batch], 'Quiet': True},\n786\t            )\n787\t            removed += len(batch) - len(resp.get('Errors', []) or
